<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blase</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blaes</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaas.html>blaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blazen.html>blazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaasje.html>blaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bladder</span>

***blad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blad.html>blad</a> (4385)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bladą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰlh̥₃oto</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰleh₃-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blad.html>blad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bladeren.html>bladeren</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bladen.html>bladen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaren.html>blaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaadje.html>blaadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>leaf <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bladeren.html>bladeren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:begonnen.html>begonnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkleuren.html>verkleuren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkele.html>enkele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reeds.html>reeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevallen.html>gevallen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>leaves</b> began to change colour already and some have already fallen off.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:olifant.html>olifant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blaadje.html>blaadje</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That elephant would like to eat a green <b>leaf</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loof.html>loof</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The normal plural for this meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bladeren.html>bladeren</a></i>. The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bladen.html>bladen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> extremely <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> and may be considered erroneous. The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:blaren.html>blaren</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dialectal or archaic and literary.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blad.html>blad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bladen.html>bladen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaadje.html>blaadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sheet of paper, leaf (in a book)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steek.html>Steek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> hand <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuw.html>nieuw</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blad.html>blad</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Raise your hand if you need a new <b>sheet of paper</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li>magazine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blad.html>blad</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lokale.html>lokale</a> podiumkunst <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelezen.html>gelezen</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have you already read that new magazine about local performing <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a>?</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">blāt</i>. Possibly related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">blé</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wheat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blamage.html>blamage</a> (42536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:blamage.html>Blamage</a></i>, originally coined in German student <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> as a pseudogallicism. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blameren.html>blameren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-age</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>A disgrace, something that tarnishes the reputation of someone or something.</li></ol>

***blameren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blameren.html>blameren</a> (76984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:blameren.html>blameren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">blasmer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*blastēmō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">blasphēmō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βλασφημέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blasphēméō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blameren.html>blameren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander, to calumniate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disgrace, to humiliate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">blasfemeren</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***blanc.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blanc.html>blanc</a> (49875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*blancus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blankaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bright, <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a>, blinding, white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bhleg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">blanch</i> "bright, white" (German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a>, white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">blankr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bright, shiny</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white, <a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">blink</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:blind.html>blind</a></span>.
</p>

***blanco.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blanco.html>blanco</a> (15710)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blankaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white, bright, blinding</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bhleg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, through a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*blancus</i>. Found as early as the Cantar <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mio.html>Mio</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cid.html>Cid</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">blanch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a>, bright, white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:blanc.html>blanc</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white, grey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:blanca.html>blanca</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white <a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i>, etc.
</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zware.html>zware</a> klimwerk <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blaren.html>blaart</a></b> hand <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voet.html>voet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The arduous climbing <b>blisters</b> both hand and foot.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To get/show blisters</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">blèren</i>. Comparable and possibly cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">plärren</i> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">blēren</i>).
</p>

</p>

***blaten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blaten.html>blaten</a> (61604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaten.html>blaten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bleten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blāten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*blātijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blētijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bleat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blaten.html>blaten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bleat, produce the typical <a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a> sound of sheep</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to speak as pointlessly as if it <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> gibberish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blaten.html>blaten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brommer.html>brommer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:interesseert.html>interesseert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reet.html>reet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>Stop</a> <b>blabbering</b> about your moped, I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> give a <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a> about that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***blauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a> (1885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blau</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blāo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*blāu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blēwaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauwer.html>blauwer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">blauwst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blue</li>
<li>visibly bruised, as in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a></b> 'a bluish <a href = vnd.unilang:bruisen.html>bruise</a>'</li>
<li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>) drunk</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>The colour blue.</li>
<li>Police (especially in the phrase: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straat.html>straat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">police on the street</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)</li></ol>

***blauwe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> (1392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>For the sense as an ethnic slur, unknown. Several <a href = vnd.unilang:theories.html>theories</a> have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> proposed, the merits of which are unclear, all of which refer to some feature of Indonesian people appearing blue to the eye. In one theory, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a supposed blue colour of their gums, while another refers to a blue <a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a> reportedly seen on the pitch-black hair of some Indonesians. Finally, yet another theory relates this to the so-called <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolian_spot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mongolian spot">slate-grey nevus</a> prevalent among new-born Austronesians. Cf. also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hap.html>hap</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a></i></span></li></ol>

***blazer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blazer.html>blazer</a> (39773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">blaze</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. Originates from the 'blazing' scarlet <a href = vnd.unilang:jackets.html>jackets</a> worn by members of Lady Margaret Boat Club, the rowing club associated with St. John's College, Cambridge. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">blæsere</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">blasere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burner, incendiary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:blazer.html>blazer</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:blazer.html>blazer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:blazers.html>blazers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A semi-formal jacket.</li>
<li>A person or thing that blazes (marks or <a href = vnd.unilang:cuts.html>cuts</a> a route).</li>
<li>Anything that blazes or glows, as with heat or flame.</li>
<li>The dish used when cooking directly <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the flame of a chafing-dish <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>, or the coals of a brazier.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:smokes.html>smokes</a> cannabis; a <a href = vnd.unilang:stoner.html>stoner</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who spreads news, or blazes <a href = vnd.unilang:matters.html>matters</a> abroad.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Edmund Spenser and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:blazers.html>blazers</a></b> of crime</dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<li>A con or swindle.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">blöe</i>, <i class="Latn <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰleh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yellow, grey, blue</span><span ***blij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a> (367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With regular loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijde.html>blijde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blide</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blīthi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blīþiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijer.html>blijer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">blijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">happy</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straten.html>straten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If the streets are white, the children are <b>happy</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">glad</span></li></ol>

***blijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijken.html>blijken</a> (6558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bliken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blīcan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blīkaną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blīkijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijken.html>blijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appear, to become apparent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>Oorspronkelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Atomium <a href = vnd.unilang:bedoeld.html>bedoeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slechts.html>slechts</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Expo <a href = vnd.unilang:overeind.html>overeind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bleek.html>bleek</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dermate.html>dermate</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:populair.html>populair</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgebroken.html>afgebroken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Originally, the Atomium <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> meant to remain standing only during the Expo, but it <b><a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> out</b> so popular that it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> never <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bliven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">blīvan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bilībaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stay, to remain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:blijf.html>Blijf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Stay</b> here, I'm going to have a look.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stay, to remain, to still be</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep/keep on, to continue to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeurt.html>gebeurt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachen.html>lachen</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Whatever <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>, always <b>keep</b> laughing!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***blik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a> (1751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blic</i>, ultimately from the root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijken.html>blijken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to appear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikje.html>blikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A glance.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>ray</a>, a beam.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:terugblik.html>terugblik</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blic</i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bleek.html>bleek</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikje.html>blikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A can, a tin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">container</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haalde.html>haalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blikje.html>blikje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:automaat.html>automaat</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She got a <b>can</b> from the vending machine.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winkeltje.html>winkeltje</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dorp.html>dorp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkocht.html>verkocht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The only shop in the village only <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> <b>canned</b> vegetables.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Sheet metal, tin plate; the metallic material tins are made of, often coated with tin or pewter.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">dustpan</span>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a> (7009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tin, <a href = vnd.unilang:tinnen.html>tinnen</a>, made of a light tinplate (or similar metallic alloy) as produced for cans
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a></b> koekjesdoos <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nostalgisch.html>nostalgisch</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>tin</b> cookie box <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a nostalgic quality.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
